> _Prior:_ 2026-07-05 by **PP-B3 RESOLVED ÔÇö 5 attributes were emitted in the WRONG PP Appendix A datatype Ôćĺ LIVE `main` + Staging**. The audit's highest-priority open item (potential PP106 whole-listing rejection) was settled with a **read-only `GetFullDetailsOfAllListingsByBranch` call against the live HFC branch (327 listings)** ÔÇö the authoritative datatype ground truth. Result: `Kitchen`(191/191 stored `"Yes"`), `Family_TV_Room`(11), `Study`(13), `StaffQuarters`(16), `Entrance_hall`(37) are all **boolean `"Yes"`** in Appendix A, but `PrivatePropertyListingMapper::buildAttributes()` emitted them as **integer counts** in the `$counts` loop ÔÇö a datatype mismatch. **Why it never visibly broke:** PP *coerces* a numeric value to `"Yes"` for boolean attributes (the ONLY reason property 6049 survived with `Kitchen="1"` ÔÇö the audit's "Kitchen is a proven count" anchor was WRONG; PP silently coerced it). The 2026-07-02 PP106s were the *reverse* mismatch (old `EnSuite="true"` boolean Ôćĺ integer attr, since fixed to `EnSuite="1"`). **Fix:** the five moved out of `$counts` into present-only `"Yes"` flags (keyed off `Kitchen`/`TV Room`/`Study`+`Office`/`Domestic Room`/`Entrance Hall` spaces); `Lounges`/`DiningAreas`/`Parking`/`Carports` stay integer counts (read-back-confirmed 1ÔÇô3). Tinker-verified: buildAttributes now emits Kitchen/Family_TV_Room/Study/StaffQuarters/Entrance_hall=`"Yes"`, Lounges/DiningAreas/Parking/Carports=int. `GetFullDetailsOfAllListingsByBranch` is the standard read-back to settle any future count-vs-flag question (WSDL op exists; called via the client's generic `call()`). Files: `PrivatePropertyListingMapper.php`, audit doc (PP-B3 Ôćĺ RESOLVED). No migration/route/perm. ÔÜá´ŞĆ live box is `--no-dev` Ôćĺ run `PpFeatureAttributesTest` on laragon.

> _Prior:_ 2026-07-05 by **SYNDICATION MAPPING FIXES (5) Ôćĺ LIVE `main` + Staging**. From the 2026-07-05 syndication-mapping audit (`.ai/audits/syndication-mapping-audit-2026-07-05.md`), the five confirmed "fix-now" items landed. **PP (`PrivatePropertyListingMapper`):** (PP-B1) `Carports` was dead code ÔÇö `countSpaces($property,'Carport')` but a carport is a FEATURE of the `Parking` space, not a space type, so it always returned 0 and never syndicated Ôćĺ new `countCarports()` sums Parking bays/units carrying the `Carport` feature (space-level featuresAll Ôçĺ bay count, else per-unit hits; tinker-proven 2/2/0). (PP-B2) `Laundry` checked `hasSpace('Laundry')` but the space type is `'Laundry Room'` Ôćĺ never fired Ôćĺ fixed. (PP-G1) seven amenity flags (Gym/Clubhouse/TennisCourt/SquashCourt/Jaccuzzi/Jetty_Berth/Storage) only checked `has()` feature strings, so entered as a SPACE they never fired Ôćĺ OR-ed the matching `hasSpace(<type>)` (Gym/Clubhouse/Tennis Court/Squash Court/Jacuzzi/Jetty/Storeroom, all verified against `config/property-spaces.php`). **P24 (`Property24ListingMapper`):** (P24-B1) `showLocation` used `(bool)($lat && $lng)` but lat/lng are `decimal:7` string casts ("0.0000000" is truthy) Ôćĺ never-geocoded listings emitted `showLocation:true` (privacy-adjacent) Ôćĺ numeric guard mirroring the proven line-82 `geographicLocation` fix. (P24-G1) `rentalInfo.rentalRate` never sent Ôćĺ weekly/daily/short-term rentals published at P24's default MONTHLY cadence Ôćĺ new `mapRentalRate()` maps `rental_price_type` Ôćĺ RentalRate enum (Month/Week/Day/Year/SquareMetre), NULL for blank/unknown so P24 keeps its own default. ÔÜá´ŞĆ LIVE `/corex` box is `composer install --no-dev` (no phpunit) Ôćĺ verification was `php -l`-clean + a bootstrapped tinker harness (Carports both shapes, all 8 space strings resolve, every rental cadence maps); the covering test files (`tests/Unit/PrivateProperty/PpFeatureAttributesTest.php`, `tests/Unit/Syndication/Property24FeatureTagsTest.php`) must be RUN on dev/laragon via `dev-check.ps1`. No migration, no route/perm/nav change. Files: `PrivatePropertyListingMapper.php`, `Property24ListingMapper.php`, audit doc. > _Prior:_ 2026-07-04 by **P24 SUBMIT-TIMEOUT HOTFIX ÔÇö a transient Property24 timeout no longer clobbers a LIVE listing to 'error' Ôćĺ LIVE `main`**. Symptom (Johan): property **1357** (ref **117201765**) showed `P24 Ref: 117201765 ÔÇö Error  Error: Connection failed: cURL error 28: Operation timed out after 120000ms with 0 bytes received` ÔÇö a listing that was STILL LIVE on the portal, mislabelled broken; **5 submit timeouts on 2026-07-04** (P24-side slowness ÔÇö 0 bytes back within the 120s read timeout; today also 16 connect-timeouts on harmless `status_check`). ROOT CAUSE: `Property24SyndicationService::performSubmit()` wrote a permanent `p24_syndication_status='error'` + the raw cURL string into `p24_last_error` on ANY save failure ÔÇö INCLUDING a transient timeout (no HTTP status). The `isTransientFailure()` classifier already existed and was correctly used by `deactivate/reactivate` (AT-P24 #5) but **never by the submit/update path**. An `error` row additionally (a) lost every UI recovery button (View/Refresh/Deactivate require active|submitted|submitting) and (b) was excluded from `syncAllActivations()` reconcile Ôćĺ **stranded**. FIX (root-cause, mirrors AT-P24 #5): `performSubmit` now branches transientÔćĺ`handleTransientSubmitFailure()` ÔÇö **has p24_ref Ôćĺ keep 'active'** (it's still live) + amber "Sync deferred ÔÇö still live; tap Refresh to retry" note; **no ref Ôćĺ 'pending'** (retryable), never a hard error. Permanent 4xx (validation) Ôćĺ unchanged crimson `error`. UI (`properties/show.blade.php`): sync-state poller no longer shows a FALSE "success" toast when a deferred note is present, and a new amber status line surfaces the note on reload (buttons stay). REMEDIATION: property 1357 verified live via a real `isOnPortal` call (`data:true`) Ôćĺ reset to `active`/enabled, error cleared. TEST: `tests/Feature/Syndication/Property24SubmitTransientFailureTest.php` (2 cases: live-listing timeout stays active / first-submit timeout Ôćĺ pending). ÔÜá´ŞĆ the LIVE `/corex` box is `composer install --no-dev` (no phpunit/collision) Ôćĺ this test must be RUN on dev/laragon via `dev-check.ps1`; here it was `php -l`-clean and the transient classification tinker-verified (timeout/503Ôćĺtransient, 422Ôćĺpermanent). Files: `Property24SyndicationService.php`, `resources/views/corex/properties/show.blade.php`, new test. No migration, no new route/perm.

> _Prior:_ 2026-06-26 by **AT-106 ÔÇö daily self-cleaning P24 location sync (stamp-and-sweep) Ôćĺ LIVE (direct to main)**. Answers "how do we keep provinces/cities/suburbs always correct so a phantom can't recur": `p24:sync-locations` now **stamps `p24_verified_at=now()` on every province/city/suburb P24 returns**, then **soft-deletes anything it did NOT return this run** (verified_at < runStart) ÔÇö and is **scheduled daily at 11:00** (`routes/console.php`, `withoutOverlapping`; the old monthly entry removed as redundant). This makes the tree self-healing: removed P24 locations (the city-tier staleness AT-105 found ÔÇö Durban North/785 etc.) get swept automatically; new ones appear. **Safety:** the full walk aborts on ANY fetch error before pruning, AND an **absolute sanity floor** (P24 must return Ôëą 5 provinces / 50 cities / 3000 suburbs) skips the sweep on a truncated/auth-broken reply so an API blip can never wipe the tree (deliberately absolute, NOT a ratio-of-current-table ÔÇö the table is bloated with stale rows the first sweep must clear). Pruned suburbs remediate dependent properties (FK chain nulled + `p24_suburb_mismatch=1`); pruned cities/provinces null the matching property FK. Soft-delete only (#1) Ôćĺ recoverable, and a returned location is revived via `withTrashed()->updateOrCreate`. **Per-agency runs do NOT prune** (`--no-prune` added to `AgencyController` cred-validation syncs + `SyncP24LocationsJob` when agency-scoped) ÔÇö only the authoritative global daily run sweeps. New `--no-prune` flag on the command. Migration `2026_06_26_140000` adds `p24_verified_at` + soft-deletes to `p24_provinces`/`p24_cities` (suburbs already had them from AT-105) + backfills existing rows. Test `P24LocationSweepTest` (healthy run sweeps only unstamped rows / floor skips on a partial run). **FIRST SWEEP DONE on live** (manual run, observed): swept **197 stale cities + 6,108 suburbs** (6,107 stale + the AT-105 phantom); now 9 provinces / 616 cities / 20,754 suburbs active, **0 active rows left unstamped**, **267/267 syndicating listings kept their `p24_suburb_id`**, **0 properties remediated** (nothing depended on a pruned location). All soft-deleted Ôćĺ recoverable. **Resilience fix (commit `0df9cf9a`):** the first attempt aborted on a single cURL-28 timeout (P24 slow on one cityId) ÔÇö by design it aborted BEFORE pruning (0 pruned, syndication intact), proving the safety. Every P24 fetch is now wrapped in `fetchRetry` (bounded exponential backoff on transient connection/5xx/429, fail-fast on definitive 4xx, still throws-before-prune if P24 is truly down). Supersedes the AT-105 "AT-106 follow-up" note (reconcile is now obsoleted by the sweep for routine upkeep; keep `p24:reconcile-suburbs` as a manual one-off). The importer page (`/admin/importer/p24-locations`) progress panel now shows a sweep summary on completion ("Swept N stale locations (X cities, Y suburbs) ┬Ě Z properties remediated", or "Sweep skipped ÔÇö tree left intact"). Commits: `ad190521` (sweep) + `cd6890c0` (schema) + `0df9cf9a` (retry) + UI line.

Collision suburb names were syndicating to the wrong P24 city ÔÇö South Coast "Glenmore" (Port Edward, p24_id 10790) listings showed as "Durban" (10787). ## 1. Identity & Stack

**Who:** Johan Reichel (CEO, HFC). Andre Roets (full-stack dev). Two-person team building CoreX OS ÔÇö real estate operating system. HFC (Home Finders Coastal) is the first live agency. Long-term vision: SA's leading real estate OS, replacing PropCon / Sage / Property24 layers across the industry.

**Stack:** Laravel 12 / Blade / Alpine.js. MySQL prod (`hfc_corex`, `hfc_staging`). SQLite local. Vite. Ubuntu on Hetzner `91.99.130.85`. Code at `/corex` (live) and `/corex-staging`. Python AI service `/opt/hf-ai/app.py` port 3100 (not in git).

**Domain:** `corex.hfcoastal.co.za` live. Staging on port 8084.

**Branches:** `main` (live), `Staging`, `HFC2402` (Johan dev), `andre` (Andre dev), feature branches off Staging. Discipline: HFC2402 + andre Ôćĺ Staging Ôćĺ staging server Ôćĺ main Ôćĺ live. Hotfix exception: direct to main, then back-sync to Staging.

**VS Code Claude** is the coding agent. Johan pastes prompts, it executes. Specs in `.ai/specs/`, read at start of every prompt.

## 1.5 Operating Principle (read this first, every chat)

CoreX is the best real estate operating system that will ever exist. This is the decision filter for every prompt, every architectural choice, every "should we ship this now" call.

- Best-in-class or rebuild ÔÇö if competitors do something better, we build ours better
- No shortcuts ever ÔÇö later does not exist; build it right the first time
- Integration is the moat ÔÇö every feature seamlessly connects to every other
- Built for agents, not screens ÔÇö we absorb complexity so they don't have to
- AI enhances, never replaces human judgement
- Constraint is fuel ÔÇö build best with what we have, never use lack of resources as an excuse

Decision test before any commit: **does this make CoreX the best, or does it make CoreX merely working?** If the answer is "working", redesign.

"Good enough for now" is never the answer. "We'll fix it later" is never the answer.

See CLAUDE.md "CoreX Operating Principle" section for the full version.

## 2. Working Rules

- **Investigate before fixing.** Every issue: (1) audit, (2) Johan approves fix approach, (3) only then fix prompt. Never guess root causes.
- **One concern per prompt.** Two only if tightly related and same file.
- **Surgical changes.** No refactoring beyond scope.
- **Every prompt opens:** read CLAUDE.md, .ai/STANDARDS.md, relevant spec, and this file.
- **Every prompt closes:** php -l, php artisan view:clear, scripts/dev-check.ps1 if structural change, Tinker verification, **update this CHAT_STARTER.md**.
- **No hard deletes.** SoftDeletes only.
- **PPRA not EAAB. POPIA consent rules apply.**
- **Bug report = code is wrong.** Never blame caching or user error.

## 4. Recent decisions log (last 15, newest top)

- **2026-07-07** ÔÇö **MIC "THIS WEEK" TILE BUTTONS FIXED Ôćĺ LIVE (main) + Staging.** Andre reported the Work-tab hero buttons (Pitch now / View pocket / See new) don't work. CAUSE 1 (the "do nothing"): tiles cached by `WarmThisWeekTilesJob` @02:30 in a queue context (no request host) Ôćĺ `route()` baked absolute `https://corexos.co.za`; `session.domain=NULL` = host-only cookies Ôćĺ agents on canonical `corex.hfcoastal.co.za` clicked Ôćĺ cross-domain nav Ôćĺ no session Ôćĺ login bounce. FIX: `ThisWeekTileBuilder` emits RELATIVE `action_url`s (`route(...,[],false)`) ÔÇö works on any domain, and the nightly job can never bake a cross-domain host again. CAUSE 2 (mismatch/empty): tile counts came from different queries than their links ÔÇö matches 4592 (raw match rows) vs `pitch_now_high` 829; new 7 (`tracked_properties` since Friday) vs `new_today` 0 Ôćĺ "See new" landed on an EMPTY list; pocket 6 (demand) vs 1 (supply). FIX: preset logic extracted to `App\Services\Prospecting\ProspectingActionPresetService` (single source of truth); `MarketIntelligenceController::applyActionPreset` delegates to it; the tile builder counts THROUGH it, mirroring work()'s `groupBy(property_group_id ?? 'single_'.id)` so the count == the rows you land on; pocket headlines supply (demand as context); any tile with an empty destination is suppressed. Live-verified for Andre: matches 829==829, pocket 1==1, new-tile correctly hidden. Cleared all `tiles:user:%` cache rows so every agent gets fresh relative-URL tiles. Test `ThisWeekTileConsistencyTest` (grouping-collapse + relative-URL). MIC spec addendum. - **2026-07-07** ÔÇö **CALENDAR BLACKOUT ROOT-FIXED Ôćĺ LIVE (main) + Staging.** Kym + all 22 HFC agents had genuinely-empty calendars (events all present in DB). CRITICAL: AT-197's impact statement ASSUMED inactive = "materialised but inert / agents keep working normally" ÔÇö but the real code returned NULL and dropped the events. Only HFC because agency 1 is the ONLY agency with agency-specific override rows, and `forAgencyAndClass()` returns an agency row even when inactive Ôćĺ the dead overrides shadowed the active globals. FIX (fix-the-class): inactive/missing class config resolves to `'neutral'` (visible, no urgency), NEVER null ÔÇö a class-config state must never ERASE an existing event; deactivating stops new-event generation+RAG+notifications only. `'neutral'` was already a valid resolved colour (beyond-green case) so zero downstream change; owners always pass `canSee` via the creator rule. REJECTED a blanket active-global fallback in `forAgencyAndClass` (would delete per-agency deactivation entirely). DATA: reactivated the 48 rows to restore RAG immediately, then reset them to global via `resetEventClass` semantics (47/48 byte-identical copies of globals = accidental shadow; `manual` differed only in notifications; ALL backed up to storage first ÔÇö model has NO SoftDeletes, so hard-delete of the thin override layer is the sanctioned "reset to global"). Test `InactiveClassStillRendersTest` (activeÔćĺRAG, inactiveÔćĺneutral, incident-shape overrideÔćĺneutral, resolve() null only when dateless). Spec ┬ž17. - **2026-06-30** ÔÇö **AT-130 ÔÇö ONE canonical OtpService (build-once OTP engine), ClientAuth migrated onto it (no second engine).** Preceded by the OTP sweep (`.ai/audits/2026-06-30-at130-otp-engine-sweep.md`): the only real OTP was ClientAuth's client-portal login (`ClientOtp` + `issueOtp/verifyOtp`); Andre's "mobile OTP" = that same one, mobile-consumed via `/api/v1/client-auth/otp/*`; `TvAccessCode` is a pairing code, not an OTP; "OTP" in esign = "Offer To Purchase". Field clear Ôćĺ build. **Engine** `App\Services\Otp\OtpService`: generate 6-digit **hashed at rest**; deliver via the **sender-only** `otp` mailer to **the consumer's destination** (never a fixed mailbox Ôćĺ break-glass-to-requester's-own-email satisfiable WITHOUT touching the mailer); validate latest unused/unexpired/matching-purpose, **single-use**, attempts++ on miss; **throttle** (resend cooldown + hourly cap) per (bucket,destination); **audit** every issue+verify to a **CONSUMER-PROVIDED sink** ÔÇö engine hard-codes NO sink and NO role/capability check (capability = consumer's concern). Defaults `config/otp.php` carried over verbatim from clientauth (6/10min/5/60s/5-per-hr), overridable per call. **Store**: generalised `client_otps` **IN PLACE** (additive, live-safe, NO rename ÔÇö seeder/test/relation reference the name) ÔÇö +`subject_type/subject_id` (generic polymorphic subject), `destination`, `channel`; backfill `destination=email`; relax legacy `email`ÔćĺNULL. `App\Models\Otp` = canonical model (table `client_otps`); `ClientOtp` now a BC subclass (keeps `ClientUser->otps()` + fixtures); `Otp::creating` mirrors `emailÔćĺdestination` for BC. **ClientAuth migrated, behaviour identical**: `issueOtp/verifyOtp` delegate to OtpService (destination=client email, subject=ClientUser, `ClientAuthOtpMail` preserved, fake-`@corexclient.co.za` skip preserved, legacy `client_user_id`+`email` still populated, `ClientAccessLog otp_sent` sink preserved); controller issuance throttle now `OtpService->throttle('client_login', email)` (bucket shared across activation+recovery = prior per-email keying). **Verify** (Tinker rolled-back tx + endpoint, NO dev-check): php -l clean; migrate up/down/up clean; schema snapshot regenerated; **Tinker 28/28 PASS** (hash-at-rest, single-use, attempt-cap, expiry, arbitrary-destination delivery, client-login parity, fake-domain skip, throttle, audit-routes-to-consumer-sink/engine-writes-nothing-to-ClientAccessLog); **`ClientAuthFlowTest` OTP 3/3** (HTTP `/otp/send`+`/otp/verify`). **RESERVED AT-132 Wave 2 (noted, NOT built):** `comms_break_glass` consumer (capability `communications.grant_access`, destination=requester's own verified email, success=thread-scoped session grant, sink=`comms_access_audit_log`; ÔÜá´ŞĆ before wiring, `CommsAccessAuditLog::EVENT_TYPES` must gain `otp_issued`+`otp_unlock` or `record()` throws). `TvAccessCode` left alone. - **2026-06-21** ÔÇö **AT-75: MIC reads the canonical match truth; "Buyer matched" is two threshold-anchored honest units.** DECISIONS: (1) The prospecting cache (`prospecting_buyer_matches`) is scored by the SHARED canonical engine `MatchingService::score` (only criteria the buyer specified contribute ÔÇö no Engine-B no-signal phantom defaults that made a near-empty wishlist score ~85 on every listing). Per Johan rule (b): price drift decays the % (never a hard cutoff), only deal-breakers hard-exclude, beds soft. No third engine ÔÇö `PropertyMatchScoringService::canonicalBestAcross()` delegates to `MatchingService`; `recomputeForBuyer` (dormant stock cache) left as-is. (2) Price-band tolerance is agency-configurable: `priceFitRatio` gains optional `$bandPct` (default 0.0 keeps every existing caller incl. Core Matches identical); prospecting passes `mic_price_band_pct` (┬▒10% default). (3) `score()` now skips the category/property_type component when the PROPERTY side is null ÔÇö CoreX "incomplete listings shouldn't be penalised" (prospecting listings carry no category; a category-specifying buyer was wrongly dragged to 62 on every listing). A present-but-different value still scores 0 (real mismatch). (4) The "Buyer matched" KPI is now TWO threshold-anchored units (agency `mic_match_threshold`, default 75%): `buyers_matched` = distinct countable buyers with a real match Ôëą threshold (this is the pipeline-reconciling number ÔÇö only countable buyers are ever cached), `properties_matched` = distinct canvass listings Ôëą threshold; tile clickable Ôćĺ worklist filtered to the band. (5) Dual-handle %-range slider reuses the presentations `review.blade.php` vanilla pattern (crossing handles, live label, navigate-on-release ÔÇö MIC filters are full-page GETs); `work()` filters the post-get collection by `score_min/score_max` + sorts `match_score` desc, per-row count floor follows the band. Staging proof (agency 1): the inflation is gone ÔÇö Larochelle's specific wishlist narrowed 7,498Ôćĺ1,485 in-band; tile = **2 buyers ┬Ě 5,293 properties ┬Ě 75%+ vs pipeline 3** (the 3rd = AT-74 no-core-match buyer) Ôćĺ reconciles. - **2026-06-21** ÔÇö **AT-74 HOTFIX: two staging bugs from Build 4.** (1) Blade does not parse an `@if` directive glued to a preceding word character (`demand@if(...)`) but DOES parse the trailing `@endif` Ôćĺ a stray endif 500'd the whole presentation page. - **2026-06-18** ÔÇö **GPS-BORROW-FIX: subject pin no longer borrows a sibling property's GPS** (same branch `feat-ss-presentation-complex-identity`; **committed locally, then pushed + deployed to `/corex-staging` via the SS-COMPLEX-IDENTITY batch FF**). Property 771 (Duke Road, Margate) rendered ~1.2 km off and showed "0 comps within 1km". ROOT CAUSE: `AddressResolverService::resolveFromMarketReports` (the market-report borrow branch) OR-ed its address-needle match with a bare `source_suburb = ?` clause, so when a suburb was known EVERY same-suburb report matched and `orderByDesc('id')` returned a sibling's `subject_latitude/longitude` ÔÇö 771 inherited Acacia Road's pin (`-30.8468120, 30.3764720`, market_reports 93/94) and it was cached as confidence `exact` (geocoding_cache row 6147 `duke road margate`), so it re-served forever. THREE-PART FIX: **(i)** an address-needle match is now REQUIRED (`if (empty($needles)) return null` ÔÇö suburb alone never borrows); the suburb clause becomes an optional CONFIRM (`source_suburb = ? OR NULL/''`) that only NARROWS a needle match so a same-street-name report in a different suburb can't be borrowed. **(ii)** `resolve()` gains a `bypassCache` param ÔÇö a re-resolve skips the cache READ but still write-throughs via `cacheAndReturn` (updateOrCreate), so a previously-poisoned entry is OVERWRITTEN instead of re-served. **(iii)** `PropertyGeoBackfillService::backfillProperty` now resolves when `pinIsSuspect()` (suburb-centroid/unresolved/low-confidence) not just on null/force, passes `bypassCache: $latLngBefore` on re-resolves, and a new `confidenceRank()` guard (exact 5 > street 4 > suburb 3 > town 2 > unknown 1 > failed 0) means a re-resolve NEVER downgrades a good pin ÔÇö replacing the old "overwrite only if null" which was itself a bug-class making any wrong coord permanent. `PresentationGeneratorService` subject-geocode trigger extended to `|| pinIsSuspect()`. **Tests:** 4 green in `tests/Feature/Geo/SubjectGpsBorrowFixTest.php` (suburb-never-borrows / address-match-beats-higher-id-sibling / suspect-self-heals-bypassing-poisoned-cache-and-upgrades / guard-never-downgrades). Two needed fixture fixes only ÔÇö `Property::create` was missing `agent_id` (Ôćĺ no-default) then `branch_id` (PropertyObserver fell back to non-existent id 1 Ôćĺ FK violation); setUp now creates a real Branch + assigns the agent's `branch_id`; the runtime logic was never the failure. **VERIFIED on hfc_staging** (ran the fixed dev code against the staging DB, `force: true`): property 771 `-30.8468120/30.3764720` (Acacia) Ôćĺ **`-30.8578220/30.3742930` (Duke Road truth, from market_report 162)**, NOT Acacia; poisoned geocoding_cache row 6147 overwritten via write-through. **FOLLOW-ON:** (a) the `/corex-staging` checkout is on branch `Staging` and does NOT carry the fix ÔÇö it must be deployed before the live property page pin/comps reflect the correction; (b) 6 `storage/tmp_*.php` scratch files (dev: marketanchor_audit/pumula_rows/pumula_sweep; staging: complabel_audit/marketanchor_audit/pumula_audit_partB) await manual deletion ÔÇö `rm` is permission-blocked in this session. Files: `AddressResolverService`, `PropertyGeoBackfillService`, `PresentationGeneratorService`, new `SubjectGpsBorrowFixTest`.

- **2026-06-15** ÔÇö **AT-36 Communication Archive ÔÇö Pending Triage (Phase A) closed out** (off AT-34). The spine's pending-grace buffer now has a staff workflow + BM audit surface, no AI. (c) **agent_vs_agent alerts fire only on cross-agent contradiction** ÔÇö Agent B flagging `real_estate` over Agent A's `not_real_estate` writes a `communication_flag_alerts` row (status open) + stamps `contradicted_at`/`contradicted_by_user_id`; an agent reversing their OWN flag is not an alert (intentional, tested). - **2026-06-12** ÔÇö **AT-22 item 2 LIVE LEAK fixed at the root ÔÇö competitor branding now blocked by IMAGE CONTENT, not just URL.** PRES 87 / v175 leaked the RE/MAX "Coast and Country" logo as the "12 Bairn Street" competitor card (PP-T5391969, prospecting_listings #1566). Fix: added an IMAGE-CONTENT layer to `ListingImageValidator` ÔÇö `inspectImageBytes()/inspectImageFile()` run tesseract OCR for competitor brand-text (`brand:remax` ÔÇŽ) + a flat-graphic colour signal (uniq-colours ÔëĄ64 AND luminance-entropy <4.0; real PP photos measured 195ÔÇô283 / 7.25ÔÇô7.50, a flat brand card 26 / 1.96 ÔÇö huge margin, near-zero false-positive). Detection runs ONCE at ingress (`DownloadListingThumbnail`, on full-res bytes) and persists to new column `prospecting_listings.thumbnail_blocked_reason`; render gate (`CompetitorStockMatchService::scoreAndMapRow`) + the `corex.market.thumbnail` route both honour it (blocked Ôćĺ "No photo" placeholder / 404). Removed the meaningless `?:` path-fallback. New backfill command `prospecting:rescan-thumbnail-brands` (--only/--dry-run/--rescan) re-inspects historic stored thumbnails ÔÇö **this is the live remediation: run it on prod to block the existing PP-T5391969 file.** Verified end-to-end against #1566: pre-fix gate `genuine=true` (LEAK) Ôćĺ post-fix `brand:remax` Ôćĺ placeholder + 404. Conservative on every tooling gap (undecodable bytes / missing tesseract Ôćĺ genuine; flat-graphic signal + URL layer still apply). LIVE NOTE: install `tesseract-ocr` on the prod host for brand-TEXT coverage; the flat-graphic signal works without it. Migration added Ôćĺ schema snapshot re-dumped. - **2026-06-10** ÔÇö **Push-notification storm fixed at the root (server-side).** A user's handset was bricked by a repeated FCM push. Root cause: two paths (`NotificationDispatcher::sendPush` + the `PushNewPortalLeadToMobile` listener) called the FCM transport directly with **zero guards** ÔÇö the portal-lead listener fanned out to every device of every agency user on every `NewPortalLeadReceived` event, and the 5-minute P24 poller could re-fire that event for the same lead; duplicate device-token rows multiplied each event into several buzzes. Named culprit: **a fan-out resolving the same device token multiple times + no idempotency/cooldown/bounded-retry**. NOT an observer save-back loop, NOT infinite retry. Fix: one guarded funnel `PushNotificationService` (token dedup Ôćĺ idempotency per (key,device) via `Cache::add` Ôćĺ hard per-device per-minute rate cap Ôćĺ bounded retry+backoff Ôćĺ stale-token prune Ôćĺ per-user/min metrics). `FcmService` reduced to a single-attempt `PushTransport` adapter; `NullPushTransport` is the no-creds fallback bound in `AppServiceProvider`. Idempotency keys are stable per logical event (pillar: `user|event|subject|hourBucket`; portal lead: `portal_lead:{id}`). `DeviceTokenController::store` hardened: one active row per physical device (supersede same token under a new user), revive soft-deleted rows via `withTrashed` (fixes a latent unique-index 500), fully idempotent. `config/push.php` tunables. 13 tests (idempotency, distinct-events, token-dedup, rate cap, retry-cap, retry-then-succeed-once, dead-token-prune, no-op transport, portal-lead storm, device-token registration). Spec `.ai/specs/push-notifications.md`. No migration Ôćĺ no schema re-dump. dev-check clean; full-suite parity confirmed (pre-existing RecipientLoop env failures unchanged).

- **2026-05-27** ÔÇö E-sign reset **Commit 4** shipped: OTHER_CONDITIONS three-layer fix. Layer C (regex tolerance): `InsertableBlockRenderer::renderUnboundMarkers()` now uses a permissive match `/~{4,}([^~]{1,200}?)~{4,}/s` + new `normalisePurposeToken()` that strips HTML, normalises case + whitespace, and fuzzy-matches against `CANONICAL_PURPOSE_TOKENS` (Levenshtein ÔëĄ 2). So `~~~~<span>Other Contitions</span>~~~~` (embedded HTML + misspelling, both observed live) resolves to `OTHER_CONDITIONS` rather than rendering literally. Layer B (freshness guard): new `MergedHtmlFreshnessGuard` service compares `template.updated_at` to `document.rendered_at` (falls back to `updated_at` proxy until a migration adds the column); when stale, re-renders the blade view, replaces `merged_html`, logs `merged_html_rerendered` to `SignatureAuditLog`. Wired into `SigningController::show()` so the signing pipeline never serves a stale snapshot when the template was edited after the document. Layer A (builder validator): CDS builder `_doSaveDraft()` runs `_validateMarkerTokens()` on the tagged HTML pre-save; same pipeline as the server (strip HTML, normalise, fuzzy match) and surfaces warnings on Alpine `markerWarnings` state. Doesn't block save (agent might legitimately use a CUSTOM token) but flags malformed cases for cleanup. New test file `OtherConditionsToleranceTest` (6 cases) + the existing `RealTemplate111EndToEndTest::test_malformed_other_conditions_marker_does_not_render_literally` flipped RED Ôćĺ GREEN. 52 regression tests still pass (158 assertions). Closes Q3 of `.ai/audits/esign-reset-investigation-2026-05-27.md`.

- **2026-05-27** ÔÇö E-sign reset **Commit 2** shipped: end-to-end test scaffold + canonical template-111 fixture. Current state: 1 sanity passes, 6 expected failures pinpoint the bugs Commits 3-5 land green against (seller_2/seller_3 render, viewer-editable scope, OTHER_CONDITIONS tolerance, canonical accessor). The integration moat that was zero-tested before B1-B3 now has a contract suite. Tests assert on `$response->getContent()` decoded ÔÇö never on service method returns.
- **2026-05-27** ÔÇö E-sign reset **Commit 1** shipped: Apply-to-All consent gate now reads `signingRequest.party_role === 'agent'` ALONE (`SigningController.php:405-419`). Closes the legal bypass identified in the audit Q4: a dispatching agent (authed user with `manage_documents`) opening a recipient's signing token no longer inherits the apply-to-all initials bypass ÔÇö that token belongs to the recipient, and per-page consent is what renders. New regression test `ApplyToAllConsentGateTest` (3 cases, 8 assertions, all passing) asserts on `isAgent: true|false` in the actual `$response->getContent()`. First of six commits closing the audit's findings.
- **2026-05-27** ÔÇö E-sign reset investigation; report at `.ai/audits/esign-reset-investigation-2026-05-27.md`. Five live runtime breaks investigated against 49/49 passing tests. Findings: (Q1) template revert ÔÇö six parallel sources of "what fields exist" (cds_json, editor_state.tags, editor_state.mappings, tagged_html, field_mappings, fields_json, blade_view) with no canonical owner; CDS builder rehydrate at `cds-builder.blade.php:1205-1257` never auto-prunes orphan tag IDs after a block deletion. (Q2) seller blocks absent from rendered HTML, not hidden ÔÇö Case A multi-cluster bailout at `RoleBlockExpansionService.php:524-542` refuses to duplicate because detector reports 2 clusters (seller_name_surname_id sits in opening paragraph, separated from the seller-address/phone/email cluster); stamps only seller_1. (Q3) `~~~~OTHER_CONDITIONS~~~~` literal ÔÇö merged_html stored when template was in a different state contains misspelled `~~~~Other Contitions~~~~` with embedded HTML span between tildes; `InsertableBlockRenderer.php:459` regex doesn't tolerate either + stale snapshot is served instead of re-rendered from live blade. (Q4) Apply-to-All bypass ÔÇö `SigningController.php:411-414` defines `$isAgent` as `(hasPermission('manage_documents') OR party_role==='agent')` so dispatching agent opening a recipient link inherits agent gate; must be `party_role==='agent'` alone. (Q5) tests use hand-crafted fixtures that don't match template 111's shape ÔÇö `BlockRendererTest`'s Case A fixture has 1 clean cluster, never exercises the bailout path; `EditableScopeTest` skips the rendering pipeline entirely (no merged_html Ôćĺ expandWithLooping Ôćĺ blade render); `InfoPanelTest` is the only feature test that hits `/sign/{token}` but asserts on sidebar substrings, never on `data-recipient-identity`/`data-viewer-editable` in `$response->getContent()`. Systemic discipline gap: integration moat (Template Ôćĺ CdsDraft Ôćĺ blade Ôćĺ WebTemplateData Ôćĺ SurfaceNormalizer Ôćĺ LetterheadRefresher Ôćĺ InsertableBlockRenderer Ôćĺ RoleBlockExpansionService Ôćĺ SigningController Ôćĺ sign.blade.php) has zero tests. Fix sequence proposed: (1) gate Apply-to-All on `party_role` ÔÇö zero blast radius; (2) end-to-end test scaffold + canonical template-111 fixture BEFORE Q2 fix; (3) fix multi-cluster bailout with largest-cluster-wins or explicit `data-role-block` markers; (4) fix OTHER_CONDITIONS with builder validation + MergedHtmlFreshnessGuard + tolerate-HTML regex; (5) source-of-truth collapse ÔÇö canonical Template::canonicalFieldMappings() accessor, deprecate parallel storage; (6) CI gate failing any pipeline-touching commit without an end-to-end test diff.
- **2026-05-26** ÔÇö B3 shipped: per-recipient editable scope at signing + server-side auth + per-recipient item counter + Case D.2 static label fix (B2.5 caveat closed) + left info panel teaching recipients the flow. Recipient loop engine complete: identity (B1) + render (B2.5) + scope (B3). Operating principle enforced: B2.5's known limitation killed in same commit per the standard. Server stamps `data-viewer-editable` per field via `RoleBlockExpansionService::stampViewerEditability()` (recipient-identity match + canonical-role-token in `editable_by`, OR agent path); signing-view JS gates on the attribute, not a name-list. `SigningController::saveWebFields()` re-derives authorisation server-side from `field_mappings`, accepts both legacy flat + new identity-wrapped payload shapes, returns 403 + writes `web_fields_save_denied` audit log on violation (DOM trust eliminated). `_computeWebCounts()` extended with a sixth bucket ÔÇö empty `[data-viewer-editable]` inputs ÔÇö so the items-remaining counter is automatically per-recipient. `RoleBlockExpansionService::rewriteCloneLabels()` walks text nodes inside each clone, rewrites indexed source labels ("Seller 2" Ôćĺ "Seller 4") to the target instance via word-boundary regex, skips `<input>/<textarea>/<select>/<option>/<script>/<style>` so user data never gets mangled. `resources/views/docuperfect/signatures/external/_info-panel.blade.php` renders the persistent left rail on `>=1024px` with a 5-step guide (config-driven from `config/docuperfect.signing_guidance`), agent contact card from `template->creator`, and Signing-as block resolved via `Template::roleDisplayLabel`. Three new test files (16 tests, 32 assertions) covering scope/audit/label-rewrite/panel; total RecipientLoop suite now 49 passing (150 assertions).
- **2026-05-26** ÔÇö B2.5 shipped: role-block auto-loop completed. Single-block templates now duplicate N times for N recipients at render ÔÇö the V1-deferral from yesterday's B2 commit is closed. Engine extension: `RoleBlockDetectionService::detectBlockBoundaries()` walks the rendered body via DOMDocument, clusters consecutive `data-field` elements by role-base, computes a clean LCA per cluster (walks up when the LCA is the field-leaf itself), and emits boundary descriptors with stable XPath handles. `RoleBlockExpansionService::expandWithLooping()` is the new entry-point: per-boundary it dispatches Case A (single-block + N recipients Ôćĺ clone the LCA N times, mangle `data-field` with `__r{n}` suffix for DOM uniqueness, stamp identity, prepend `<h4 class="recipient-block-header">{Template::roleDisplayLabel(...)}: {signer}</h4>`, pre-fill each clone's spans from the recipient's `contact_id` via a sub-nameÔćĺcolumn map covering name/id/phone/email/address), Case B (max_idx == N Ôćĺ stamp only, B2 behaviour intact), Case C (single-block + 1 recipient Ôćĺ stamp only, singleton header), Case D.1 (K > N hardcoded Ôćĺ stamp N, orphan-mark K-N), Case D.2 (K < N hardcoded Ôćĺ stamp K, attempt to isolate the idx=K sub-block and auto-duplicate K+1..N; falls back to stamp+warning when the per-instance subtree can't be isolated). Wired into `SigningController::show()` replacing `stampIdentities()`. 21 tests passing (9 new B2.5 cases ÔÇö A/B/C/D.1/D.2, DOM uniqueness, per-instance prefill, mixed-role isolation, rentals labels). Tinker walk against template 347 (4-block hardcoded + 2 sellers): identical output to yesterday's B2 baseline (Case D.1 path, no duplication). Architecture matches the locked spec ÔÇö agency authors ONE role block, engine loops; hardcoded numbered templates continue to render unchanged. Known limitation: Case D.2 clones retain static index labels from the source block (e.g. an inner `<h4>Seller 2</h4>` clones to "Seller 4" instance verbatim); structural warning surfaces it. B3 (per-recipient editable scope) is next.
- **2026-05-26** ÔÇö B1 shipped: indexed recipient identity. `role_index` column added to `signature_requests` (NOT `signature_template_recipients` ÔÇö B0 had table name wrong; corrected in commit message) with PHP-regex backfill that split 84 `seller_2` rows into clean `seller` + role_index=2. `SignatureRequest` model gains `role_identity` accessor + `forRoleInstance(role, idx)` scope. `Template::mapSigningPartyKeys()` extended to auto-number duplicates while leaving singletons unchanged (backward compat). New `Template::roleDisplayLabel()` per-token helper recognises wizard's raw tokens (`seller`/`lessor`/`landlord`/`tenant`) in addition to canonical `owner_party`/`acquiring_party`. Wizard's `:1924-1937` keeps the legacy suffixed party_key string for 8 downstream callers but `SignatureService::createSigningRequest()` splits the suffix at insert so the persisted column is always clean. `SigningController::show()` now exposes `$currentRecipient` + `$currentRoleIdentity` to the view (foundation for B2 renderer + B3 signing scope). 13 tests passing. Tinker walk against live session 249 confirmed JohanÔćĺagent_1, JamesÔćĺseller_1, SteveÔćĺseller_2.
